Gentle reminder: workplace humor boundaries I’ve noticed a pattern in recent team messages where light-hearted puns and wordplay are being shared as daily icebreakers. While we value camaraderie, we must ensure these exchanges don’t create discomfort, especially for new hires or those from cultures where such humor is less common. What feels like harmless fun to one person can be perceived as unprofessional by another. Let’s keep humor inclusive and context-aware.

Humor is fine, but clarity matters when misalignment affects morale.
